Comment: tardis.kiss said "♢
☆ I used: 8B Derwent Graphic 12 Pencils, Prismacolour Coloured Pencils, Prismacolour silver & gold metallic pens, and a Gelly Roll gel pen☆
.
☆Trades, requests, collaborations, and commissions are closed☆
.
My grandmother asked me to draw this for her friend as an Easter gift.
I'm pretty happy with the way this turned out! It took about 3-4 hours, but it was worth it.
Aghh I really wish I could keep this because I'm very proud of how it turned out, but I'm hoping that my grandma's friend will enjoy it just as much. Hopefully she'll like it!
//
#easter #easterbunny #art #bunny #happyeaster #myart"

Comment: themusicroomatmidway said "Super excited to be playing "The Amazing Note Race" with third grade today!! We have been learning about the note names on the treble staff, and today we are reviewing by playing this awesome game. The kids will be in two teams. While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"

While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"
